- ...

### Decision
TRADE or HOLD (default HOLD if no edge)

## 2026-04-28 -- Pre-market Research

### Account
- Equity: $100,000.00
- Cash: $100,000.00
- Buying power: $200,000.00
- Daytrade count: 0
- Positions: 0 | Open orders: 0 (Day 1 -- fresh launch)

### Market Context
- WTI / Brent: WTI rallying (+2.84% Apr 27, June contract); Brent ~$96/bbl. Stalled US-Iran talks driving bid; Strait of Hormuz risk premium back.
- S&P 500 futures: ESM26 ~7,221 (-0.06% to flat premarket). SPX closed 7,173.91 record. Polymarket 65-66% odds of down open.
- VIX: 18.36 (Apr 27 close). Calm but creeping up from 18.02 prior.
- Today's catalysts: SOX 18-day win streak +44% since 3/31 (longest in index history, extreme overbought). US-Iran geopolitical risk. Big Tech earnings later in week. FOMC ahead.
- Earnings before open: No US names BMO. Quiet day.
- Economic calendar: No CPI/PPI/FOMC/NFP today. CPI 5/12, NFP 5/8.
- Sector momentum: Energy leads YTD (+26%), Staples (+10%), Industrials (+9.6%). Tech/Comms/Discretionary/Financials lagging on rotation -- but SOX is the outlier with parabolic move.

### Trade Ideas
1. XLE (Energy ETF) -- catalyst: Iran tensions + oil breakout + sector leadership. Entry ~current open, stop -7%, target +15%, R:R 2:1. Diversified energy exposure.
2. XOM -- catalyst: oil rally beneficiary, defensive megacap energy. Entry ~current, 10% trail stop, target +12%. Cleaner than levered E&P names on geopolitical fakeout risk.
3. PASS on semis (NVDA/SMH/SOXX): SOX +44% in 18 sessions, most extended vs 200dma since 2000. FOMO chase; awful R:R here.

### Risk Factors
- Day 1: no edge from running a system, baseline cash is correct stance.
- SPX at all-time highs; Polymarket leans down open.
- Iran headline risk cuts both ways (de-escalation gap-down in oil names).
- Big Tech earnings later this week could whip indices.
- Account loaded as $100k, not strategy doc's $10k -- size positions in % terms regardless.

### Decision
HOLD. Day 1, no positions, no urgent edge. Energy is the cleanest setup but it's already extended +26% YTD; prefer to wait for a pullback or confirm the breakout sustains a session before deploying capital. Patience > activity. Will reassess at midday and market-open routines.

But trend has clearly cracked -- if oil breaks $99 cleanly today, energy thesis weakens further; trails will catch us at -10% from hwm. Accept the planned exit if it triggers. Each is already at cap; any add lifts the position to ~30% concentration. Adds also contradicted the same entry's Trade Ideas section ("NO NEW ADDS. Energy correction in motion = catching falling knife"). SKIPPED both at market-open. Holding XLE/XOM as-is; trails are 6.7-6.8% below current (XLE $53.85 vs $57.80; XOM $140.12 vs $150.25) -- well clear of 3% rule, no manual move. Both above -7% manual cut (XLE -1.1%, XOM -1.2% from entry). Let trails handle downside; reassess at midday on WTI/Hormuz tape. Weekly slots 0/3 untouched.
